FNV GRAPHICS CAMERA MATRIX CONTRACT AUDIT

Questions:
1. Are NiCamera world-to-camera and frustum offsets proven by FNV code?
2. Are near/far values at +0xEC/+0xF0 the same values as the frustum near/far fields?
3. Is pCurrentCamera valid immediately before ProcessImageSpaceShaders for sun projection?
4. Which camera writer function is safest to mirror for CPU-side view/projection constants?

======================================================================
CAMERA MATRIX CONTRACT TO PROVE
======================================================================
Candidate layout from prior audits/TESReloaded-style reading:
  NiCamera::WorldToCam candidate: Camera + 0x94
  NiCamera::Frustum candidate: Camera + 0xD4
  NiFrustum left/right/top/bottom/near/far: +0x00/+0x04/+0x08/+0x0C/+0x10/+0x14
  Current near/far reads used by Psycho: Camera + 0xEC and Camera + 0xF0

Do not implement sun screen projection until this script proves these offsets in FNV code.
